If the air is lost to XV5004/XV6004 (loss of plant air, incorrect isolation or a split airline) the valve will be forced open due to the weight of the contents and open, potentially draining the mill contents onto the ground, resulting in significant media lose, and production lose depending on the number of mills operating.\nThe set up would be better if the manual pinch valve was located after XV5004/6004, then it could be closed after the media/ part contents of the mill has been drain. These valves could be swapped around in the ongoing routine rebuilds.
